##  clock 

 Gender = _female_;  Process (a) = *pef*; Process (b) = _clock_
<table>
 <thead>
  <tr>
   <th style="text-align:center;"> process </th>
   <th style="text-align:left;"> label </th>
   <th style="text-align:right;"> a </th>
   <th style="text-align:right;"> ae </th>
